<script type="text/javascript" charset="utf-8" language="javascript" date-src="/js_sc/cookie/" blzexc="1">
//<![CDATA[
/*\
 |*|
 |*|  :: cookies.js ::
 |*|
 |*|  A complete cookies reader/writer framework with full unicode support.
 |*|
 |*|  https://developer.mozilla.org/en-US/docs/DOM/document.cookie
 |*|
 |*|  Syntaxes:
 |*|
 |*|  * docCookies.setItem(name, value[, end[, path[, domain[, secure]]]])
 |*|  * docCookies.getItem(name)
 |*|  * docCookies.removeItem(name[, path])
 |*|  * docCookies.hasItem(name)
 |*|  * docCookies.keys()
 |*|
 \*/

var docCookies = {
  getItem: function (sKey) {
    if (!sKey || !this.hasItem(sKey)) { return null; }
    return unescape(document.cookie.replace(new RegExp("(?:^|.*;\\s*)" + escape(sKey).replace(/[\-\.\+\*]/g, "\\$&") + "\\s*\\=\\s*((?:[^;](?!;))*[^;]?).*"), "$1"));
  },
  setItem: function (sKey, sValue, vEnd, sPath, sDomain, bSecure) {
    if (!sKey || /^(?:expires|max\-age|path|domain|secure)$/i.test(sKey)) { return; }
    var sExpires = "";
    if (vEnd) {
      switch (vEnd.constructor) {
        case Number:
          sExpires = vEnd === Infinity ? "; expires=Tue, 19 Jan 2038 03:14:07 GMT" : "; max-age=" + vEnd;
          break;
        case String:
          sExpires = "; expires=" + vEnd;
          break;
        case Date:
          sExpires = "; expires=" + vEnd.toGMTString();
          break;
      }
    }
    document.cookie = escape(sKey) + "=" + escape(sValue) + sExpires + (sDomain ? "; domain=" + sDomain : "") + (sPath ? "; path=" + sPath : "") + (bSecure ? "; secure" : "");
  },
  removeItem: function (sKey, sPath) {
    if (!sKey || !this.hasItem(sKey)) { return; }
    document.cookie = escape(sKey) + "=; expires=Thu, 01 Jan 1970 00:00:00 GMT" + (sPath ? "; path=" + sPath : "");
  },
  hasItem: function (sKey) {
    return (new RegExp("(?:^|;\\s*)" + escape(sKey).replace(/[\-\.\+\*]/g, "\\$&") + "\\s*\\=")).test(document.cookie);
  },
  keys: /* optional method: you can safely remove it! */ function () {
    var aKeys = document.cookie.replace(/((?:^|\s*;)[^\=]+)(?=;|$)|^\s*|\s*(?:\=[^;]*)?(?:\1|$)/g, "").split(/\s*(?:\=[^;]*)?;\s*/);
    for (var nIdx = 0; nIdx < aKeys.length; nIdx++) { aKeys[nIdx] = unescape(aKeys[nIdx]); }
    return aKeys;
  }
};
//]]>
</script>

<script type="text/javascript" charset="utf-8" language="javascript" date-src="/js_sc/product/rosettastone/common/" blzexc="1">
//<![CDATA[
Number.prototype.digitizing = function () {
    var _num = parseFloat(this);
    if (isNaN(_num)) return this;

    var temp = _num.toString().split('.');
    temp[0] = temp[0].toString().replace(/(\d+?)(?=(?:\d{3})+$)/g, '$1,')
    return temp.join('.');
};

//]]>
</script>

var urlOption = (function () {
    var temp = {};
    if (mySearch = window.location.search.toString().replace(/^\?/, '').split('&')) {
        for (var _i = 0; mySearch.length > _i; _i++) {
            if (mySearch[_i].split("=")) {
                temp[mySearch[_i].split("=")[0]] = decodeURIComponent(mySearch[_i].split("=")[1]);
            }
        }
    }
    return temp;
})();
if(typeof URLargument === 'undefined') URLargument = urlOption;
/*****************************************************
時間制限メッセージ
TimeMessage(start,end,str,ID)

start以上end未満の間　メッセ時を出力する
start	：開始日時　yyyymmddhh
end		：終了日時　yyyymmddhh
str		：表示文字列
ID		：DOM　ID
******************************************************/
function TimeCheck(start, end) {
    var start = (typeof (start) == 'number') ? start : 0;
    var end = (typeof (end) == 'number') ? end : 9999999999;
    var mytime = (urlOption.time) ? urlOption.time : time;
    try {
        if (mytime.indexOf(":") >= 0) {
            mytime = mytime.replace(/%20/, ' ');
            var mytimeAr = mytime.split(":");
            mytime = mytimeAr[0].replace(/[^0-9]/ig, '');
        }
    } catch (e) {
    }
    return (start <= mytime && end > mytime) ? 1 : 0;
}
function TimeMessage(start, end, str, ID) {
    if (TimeCheck(start, end)) {
        if (ID) {
            if (typeof ID === "object") {
                var $obj = jQuery(ID);
                $obj.html(str);
            } else if (ID === "return") {
                return str;
            } else {
                jQuery('#' + ID).html(str);
            }
        } else {
            document.write(str);
        }
    } else {
        if (ID == 'return') {
            return '';
        }
    }
}
/*****************************************************
ページ内ポップアップ
modal_window(uri,[width,height])
uri		= 表示URL（必須）
width	= Window幅
height	= Window高さ
******************************************************/
function modal_window(uri, width, height) {
    var width = (width) ? width : 600;
    var height = (height) ? height : 400;

    var windowWidth = (function () {
        if (window.innerWidth) {
            return window.innerWidth;
        }
        else if (document.documentElement && document.documentElement.clientWidth != 0) {
            return document.documentElement.clientWidth;
        } else if (document.body) {
            return document.body.clientWidth;
        }
        return 800;
    })();
    var windowHeight = (function () {
        if (window.innerWidth) {
            return window.innerHeight;
        }
        else if (document.documentElement && document.documentElement.clientHeight != 0) {
            return document.documentElement.clientHeight;
        } else if (document.body) {
            return document.body.clientHeight;
        }
        return 600;
    })();

    height = (windowHeight * 0.8 > height) ? height : Math.ceil(windowHeight * 0.8);
    width = (windowWidth * 0.8 > width) ? width : Math.ceil(windowWidth * 0.8);

    var userAgent = window.navigator.userAgent.toLowerCase();
    var appVersion = window.navigator.appVersion.toLowerCase();


    if (userAgent.indexOf("msie") >= 0 && appVersion.indexOf("msie 6.") >= 0) {
        if (uri) {
            var nwin = window.open(uri, 'nwin', 'toolbar=no,location=no,directories=no,status=no,menubar=no,scrollbars=yes,resizable=yes,WIDTH=' + width + ',HEIGHT=' + height);
            nwin.focus();
        }
    } else if (userAgent.indexOf("iphone") >= 0 || userAgent.indexOf("ipod") >= 0 || userAgent.indexOf("android") >= 0) {
        if (uri) {
            var nwin = window.open(uri, 'nwin', 'toolbar=no,location=no,directories=no,status=no,menubar=no,scrollbars=yes,resizable=yes,WIDTH=' + width + ',HEIGHT=' + height);
            nwin.focus();
        }
    } else if (uri) {
        var innerPopup_CloseBtn = {
            "TAG": "img",
            "src": "/~/media/Images/Common/innerPopup/close",
            "width": "75",
            "height": "30",
            "alt": "閉じる"
        }
        var innerPopup_OpenBtn = {
            "TAG": "img",
            "src": "/~/media/Images/Common/innerPopup/open",
            "width": "145",
            "height": "30",
            "alt": "別ウィンドウで開く"
        }

        var innerPopup_topBAR = {
            "TAG": "div",
            "id": "innerPopup_topBAR"
        }
        var innerPopup_topBARbox = {
            "TAG": "div",
            "id": "innerPopup_topBARbox"
        }

        var innerPopup_BoxTBL = {
            "TAG": "table",
            "id": "innerPopup_base",
            "cellpadding": "0",
            "cellspacing": "0"
        };
        var innerPopup_BoxTbody = {
            "TAG": "tbody"
        }
        var innerPopup_BoxTR = {
            "TAG": "tr"
        };
        var innerPopup_BoxTD = {

            "vAlign": "middle",
            "align": "center"
        };

        var innerPopup_Frame = {

            "frameborder": "0",
            "framespacing": "0",
            "allowtransparency": "false",
            "hspace": "0",
            "vspace": "0",
            "marginheight": "0",
            "marginwidth": "0"
        };

        var elm_innerPopup_BoxTBL = makeDOM(innerPopup_BoxTBL);
        var elm_innerPopup_BoxTbody = makeDOM(innerPopup_BoxTbody);
        var elm_innerPopup_BoxTR = makeDOM(innerPopup_BoxTR);
        var elm_innerPopup_BoxTD = makeDOM(innerPopup_BoxTD);

        var elementBody = document.getElementsByTagName('body')[0];

        elm_innerPopup_BoxTBL.appendChild(elm_innerPopup_BoxTbody);
        elm_innerPopup_BoxTbody.appendChild(elm_innerPopup_BoxTR);
        elm_innerPopup_BoxTR.appendChild(elm_innerPopup_BoxTD);

        var elm_innerPopup_FrameBox = makeDOM(innerPopup_FrameBox);
        var elm_innerPopup_FrameDiv = makeDOM(innerPopup_FrameDiv);
        var elm_innerPopup_Frame = makeDOM(innerPopup_Frame);

        elm_innerPopup_FrameBox.style.width = width + "px";
        elm_innerPopup_FrameBox.style.height = height + "px";

        elm_innerPopup_Frame.src = uri;
        elm_innerPopup_Frame.border = 0;
        elm_innerPopup_Frame.frameborder = 0;
        elm_innerPopup_Frame.sandbox = 'allow-forms allow-scripts allow-top-navigation allow-same-origin';

        var elm_closeBtn = makeDOM(innerPopup_CloseBtn);
        var elm_openBtn = makeDOM(innerPopup_OpenBtn);
        var elm_innerPopup_topBAR = makeDOM(innerPopup_topBAR);
        var elm_innerPopup_topBARbox = makeDOM(innerPopup_topBARbox);

        elm_innerPopup_topBARbox.appendChild(elm_openBtn);
        elm_innerPopup_topBARbox.appendChild(elm_closeBtn);
        elm_innerPopup_topBAR.appendChild(elm_innerPopup_topBARbox);

        elm_innerPopup_FrameDiv.appendChild(elm_innerPopup_Frame);
        elm_innerPopup_FrameBox.appendChild(elm_innerPopup_topBAR);
        elm_innerPopup_FrameBox.appendChild(elm_innerPopup_FrameDiv);
        elm_innerPopup_BoxTD.appendChild(elm_innerPopup_FrameBox);

        elementBody.appendChild(elm_innerPopup_BoxTBL);

        elm_innerPopup_BoxTBL.onclick = function () {
            elementBody.removeChild(elm_innerPopup_BoxTBL);
        }
        elm_closeBtn.onclick = function () {
            elementBody.removeChild(elm_innerPopup_BoxTBL);
        }
        elm_openBtn.onclick = function () {
            elementBody.removeChild(elm_innerPopup_BoxTBL);
            var nwin = window.open(uri, 'nwin', 'toolbar=no,location=no,directories=no,status=no,menubar=no,scrollbars=yes,resizable=yes,WIDTH=' + width + ',HEIGHT=' + height);
            nwin.focus();
        }

        elm_closeBtn.onmouseout = function () {
            this.src = "/~/media/Images/Common/innerPopup/close";
        }
        elm_closeBtn.onmouseover = function () {
            this.src = "/~/media/Images/Common/innerPopup/close_on";
        }
        elm_openBtn.onmouseout = function () {
            this.src = "/~/media/Images/Common/innerPopup/open";
        }
        elm_openBtn.onmouseover = function () {
            this.src = "/~/media/Images/Common/innerPopup/open_on";
        }

    }
}

/*****************************************************
ページ内ポップアップ
open_window(uri,[width,height])
uri		= 表示URL（必須）
width	= Window幅
height	= Window高さ
******************************************************/
function open_window(uri, width, height) {
    if (window.nwin) {
        window.nwin.close();
    }
    var width = width || 720;
    var height = height || 540;
    nwin = window.open(uri, "nwin", "toolbar=no,location=no,directories=no,status=no,menubar=no,scrollbars=yes,resizable=yes,WIDTH=" + width + ",HEIGHT=" + height);
    window.nwin.focus();
}
/*****************************************************
ページ内ポップアップ
open_window(uri,[width,height])
uri		= 表示URL（必須）
width	= Window幅
height	= Window高さ
******************************************************/
function openwin(uri) {
    open_window(uri);
}
/*****************************************************
ページ内ポップアップ
open_window(uri,[width,height])
uri		= 表示URL（必須）
width	= Window幅
height	= Window高さ
******************************************************/
function popup(uri) {
    open_window(uri);
}
/*****************************************************
DOM作成
makeDOM(obj)
obj = {
"TAG":"タグ",		//省略時DIVタグ
"ID":"ID",			//ID　省略可
"myClass":"CLASS",	//Class　省略可
"myClass":"text",	//テキスト（HTML不可）
"****":"hoge"		//****で属性を作成し、値をその属性に入れる。
}
******************************************************/
function makeDOM(obj) {
    if (obj.TAG == "clear") {
        obj.TAG = 'div';
        obj.myClass = 'clear';
    }
    var myTAG = (obj.TAG) ? obj.TAG : "div";
    var temp = document.createElement(obj.TAG);
    for (var arg in obj) {
        if (arg == 'TAG') {
        } else if (arg == 'ID') {
            temp.setAttribute("id", obj.id);
        } else if (arg == 'id') {
            temp.setAttribute("id", obj.id);
        } else if (arg == 'myClass') {
            if (document.all) {
                temp.setAttribute("className", obj.myClass);
                temp.setAttribute("class", obj.myClass);
            } else {
                temp.setAttribute("class", obj.myClass);
            }
        } else if (arg == 'text') {
            var txtNode = document.createTextNode(obj.text);
            temp.appendChild(txtNode);
        } else {
            if (obj[arg]) {
                temp.setAttribute(arg, obj[arg]);
            }
        }
    }
    return temp;
}
/*****************************************************
ダウンロードサイズ
sizeWindow(size(num))
******************************************************/
function sizeWindow(num) {
    if (num) {
        open_window("//www.sourcenext.com/dl/simulation.html?" + num, 465, 360);
    } else {
        open_window("//www.sourcenext.com/dl/simulation.html", 465, 360);
    }
}
/*****************************************************
折りたたみ
exMenu(ID)

入力されたID属性の表示非表示を変更する。
該当するIDが存在しない場合は「IDが存在しません」とアラートをたてる。

ID		: CSS ID属性値（必須）
******************************************************/
function exMenu(ID) {
    var $ = jQuery;
    var $elementObj = null;
    if (typeof ID == "object") {
        $elementObj = $(ID);
    } else if ($("#" + ID) != null) {
        $elementObj = $("#" + ID);
    }
    if ($elementObj) {
        var display = $elementObj.css("display");
        var height = $elementObj.css("height");
        if (display === 'none') {
            $elementObj.css({
                overflow: 'visible',
                display: 'block',
                height: 'auto'
            });
        } else if (height === '0px' || height === '1px') {
            $elementObj.css({
                overflow: 'visible',
                height: 'auto'
            });
        } else {
            $elementObj.css({
                overflow: 'hidden',
                height: 0
            });
        }
    }
}
/********************************************/
/*		   	イメージ拡大				*/
/********************************************/
function popUp_IMG(element, tgl, img, offsetX, offsetY) {
    $img = img;
    $elm = element;
    var offset = $elm.offset();
    var _x = -(($img.outerWidth() - $elm.outerWidth()) * 0.5 - (offsetX || 0));
    var _y = -(($img.outerHeight() - $elm.outerHeight()) * 0.5 - (offsetY || 0));
    var _pos = (tgl) ? {
        "x": offset.left + _x + "px",
        "y": offset.top + _y + "px"
    } : {
        "x": "-999px",
        "y": "-990px"
    };
    $img.css({
        top: _pos.y,
        left: _pos.x,
        zIndex: 1000000000000
    });
}
function _imgPOPUP() {
    var $ = jQuery;
    var _ID = new Number();
    return function (element) {
        var $elm = $(element);
        if (mobile) { }
        else if ($elm.hasClass('nopopup')) { }
        else {
            var imgURL = $elm.attr('data-blzsrc') || $elm.attr('src');
            console.log(_ID + ' : ' + imgURL)
            var $imgBOX = $('<div />');
            $('<img />')
				.attr('id', 'IMG_p' + _ID)
				.attr('data-ImgId', _ID)
				.attr('src', imgURL)
				.appendTo($imgBOX);
            $imgBOX
				.css({ overflow: 'hidden' })
				.attr('id', 'x' + _ID)
				.attr('data-ImgSrc', imgURL)
				.attr('data-ImgId', _ID)
				.mouseout(function () {
				    var $this = $(this);
				    popUp_IMG($this, false, $this);
				})
				.appendTo('#popupIMG_TMP');
            $elm
				.attr('id', 'IMG_x' + _ID)
				.attr('data-ImgId', _ID)
				.mousemove(function () {
				    var $this = $(this);
				    var imgID = $this.attr('data-ImgId');
				    var $preloadImage = $('#IMG_p' + imgID);
				    var $imgDivId = $('#x' + imgID);
				    var time = new Date();
				    $imgDivId
						.css({
						    width: $preloadImage.outerWidth(),
						    height: $preloadImage.outerHeight()
						});
				    if ($preloadImage.outerWidth() != $elm.outerWidth()) {
				        $elm.css({ cursor: 'pointer' });
				        popUp_IMG($this, true, $imgDivId);
				    }
				    else {
				        $elm.css({ cursor: 'auto' });
				    }
				});
        }
        _ID++;
    };
}

<script type="text/javascript" charset="utf-8" language="javascript" date-src="/js_sc/jq_plugin/sn-scroll_check/" blzexc="1">
//<![CDATA[
/*
options = {
'class name':[$(startElement),$(endElement)]
};
endElement　は省略可能。
その場合、startElementのBOTTOMが値となる
$(startElement)は 'page-top' / 0 / '0' と指定することで、座標0 を指定できる。
$(endElement)は　'page-end'　を指定することで、ページの最大長さを指定できる（事実上、scrollアウトで解除しない）
*/
jQuery.fn.sn_scroll_check = function (options, offset, byElement) {
    var $ = jQuery;
    var offset = (typeof offset === 'undefined') ? 0 : offset;
    var settings = $.extend({}, options);
    var $elements = this;
    var scroll = {};
    var scrollCheck = function ($element, UID) {
        if (typeof scroll[UID] === 'undefined') scroll[UID] = 0;

        var scrollTop = $element.scrollTop() + offset;
        $target = $element;
        if (typeof $element.context === 'undefined') $target = $('body').eq(0);
        $target.addClass('target');
        var timer;
        $.each(settings, function (key, value) {
            var top, bottom;
            if (typeof byElement === 'undefined') {
                top = value[0];
                bottom = value[1];
            } else {
                if (value[0] === 'page-top' || value[0] === 0 || value[0] === '0') {
                    top = 0;
                } else {
                    var offset_1 = value[0].offset();
                    top = (typeof offset_1 === 'undefined') ? undefined : offset_1.top;
                }
                if (value[1] === 'page-end') {
                    bottom = document.documentElement.scrollHeight || document.body.scrollHeight;
                } else if (typeof value[1] !== 'undefined') {
                    var offset_2 = value[1].offset();
                    bottom = offset_2.top;
                } else {
                    bottom = offset_1.top + value[0].outerHeight();
                }
            }

            if (typeof top !== 'undefined' && typeof bottom !== 'undefined' && top <= scrollTop && bottom > scrollTop) {
                $target.addClass(key);
            } else {
                $target.removeClass(key);
            }
        });
        if (scroll[UID] > scrollTop) $target.addClass('reverse');
        else $target.removeClass('reverse');
        scroll[UID] = scrollTop;
    };
    $elements.each(function () {
        var UID = 'UID-' + Math.floor(Math.random() * 1000000000000);
        var $element = $(this);
        var UIDs = [];
        if (typeof $element.attr('data-uid') !== 'undefined') UIDs = $element.attr('data-uid').split(',');
        UIDs.push(UID);

        $element
            .attr('data-uid', UIDs.join(','))
            .on('scroll', function () {
                for (var i = 0; UIDs.length > i; i++) {
                    var UID = UIDs[i];
                    scrollCheck($(this), UID);
                }
            });
    });
    return this;
};

//]]>
</script>

<script type="text/javascript" charset="utf-8" language="javascript" date-src="/js_sc/jq_plugin/sn-youtube-popup/sn-youtube-popup/" blzexc="1">
//<![CDATA[
jQuery.fn.videoBox = function (option) {
    var $ = jQuery;
    var $elements = $(this);
    $elements.each(function () {
        var $this = $(this);
		var src = $this.data('mvurl') || $this.data('popupurl');
		var className = (typeof option !== 'undefined' && typeof option.className !== 'undefined')? option.className : 'mv-popup-anchor';
		console.log(className);
		if(typeof src === 'undefined' && className !== 'mv-popup-anchor') src = $this.attr('src');
		else if(typeof src === 'undefined') src = '//www.youtube.com/watch?v=' +($this.attr('src').split('/')[4]);
		console.log(src);
		
        $this.wrap('<a href="' + src + '" target="_blank" class="' + className + ' popup-anchor"></a>');
    });
    $('.popup-anchor').magnificPopup({
        type: 'iframe',
        iframe: {
            markup: '<div class="mfp-iframe-scaler">\n\
	<div class="mfp-close" />\n\
	<iframe class="mfp-iframe" frameborder="0" allowfullscreen />\n\
	<div class="mfp-title">Some caption</div>\n\
</div>',
            patterns: {
                youtube: {
                    index: 'youtube.com/',
                    id: 'v=',
                    src: '//www.youtube.com/embed/%id%?autoplay=1&amp;rel=0&amp;showinfo=0'
                }
            },
            srcAction: 'iframe_src'
        },
        gallery: {
            enabled: true
        },
        callbacks: {
            markupParse: function (template, values, item) {
                values.title = item.el.attr('title');
            }
        },
        disableOn: function () {
            if ($(window).width() < 480) {
                return false;
            }
            return true;
        }
    });
/*
	$('.im-popup-anchor').magnificPopup({
        type: 'iframe',
		mainClass: 'mfp-fade',
		removalDelay: 200,
		preloader: false,
		fixedContentPos: false,
        gallery: {
            enabled: true
        },
        disableOn: function () {
            if ($(window).width() < 480) {
                return false;
            }
            return true;
        }
    });
*/
    return this;
};

<script type="text/javascript" charset="utf-8" language="javascript" date-src="/js_sc/Modules/prototype/Date/" blzexc="1">
//<![CDATA[
// JavaScript Document
Date.prototype.format = function (format) {
	format = format.replace(/AAA/g, new Array('日','月','火','水','木','金','土')[this.getDay()]);
	format = format.replace(/YYYY/g, this.getFullYear());
	format = format.replace(/MM/g, ('0' + (this.getMonth() + 1)).slice(-2));
	format = format.replace(/DD/g, ('0' + this.getDate()).slice(-2));
	format = format.replace(/hh/g, ('0' + this.getHours()).slice(-2));
	format = format.replace(/mm/g, ('0' + this.getMinutes()).slice(-2));
	format = format.replace(/ss/g, ('0' + this.getSeconds()).slice(-2));
	format = format.replace(/YY/g, this.getFullYear().toString().slice(-2));
	format = format.replace(/M/g, (this.getMonth() + 1));
	format = format.replace(/D/g, this.getDate());
	format = format.replace(/h/g, this.getHours());
	format = format.replace(/m/g, this.getMinutes());
	format = format.replace(/s/g, this.getSeconds());
    return format;
};
Date.prototype.formatt = function (format) {
	return this.format(format);
}
Date.prototype.AddDays = function (days) {
	days = parseFloat(days);
	this.setDate(this.getDate() + days);
	return this;
};
Date.prototype.AddHours = function (hours) {
	hours = parseFloat(hours);
	this.setHours(this.getHours() + hours);
	return this;
};
Date.prototype.AddMinutes = function (minutes) {
	minutes = parseFloat(minutes);
	this.setMinutes(this.getMinutes() + minutes);
	return this;
};
Date.prototype.AddSeconds = function (seconds) {
	seconds = parseFloat(seconds);
	this.setSeconds(this.getSeconds() + seconds);
	return this;
};
//]]>
</script>

<script type="text/javascript" charset="utf-8" language="javascript" date-src="/js_sc/Modules/prototype/Number_digitizing/" blzexc="1">
//<![CDATA[
Number.prototype.digitizing = function () {
    var _num = parseFloat(this);
    if (isNaN(_num)) return this;

    var temp = _num.toString().split('.');
    temp[0] = temp[0].toString().replace(/(\d+?)(?=(?:\d{3})+$)/g, '$1,')
    return temp.join('.');
};
//]]>
</script>

<script type="text/javascript" charset="utf-8" language="javascript" date-src="/js_sc/jq_plugin/sn-cart/" blzexc="1">
//<![CDATA[
jQuery.fn.cartInfo = function() {
	var getValue = function (field ,format ,Value) {
		switch (field) {
			case 'SalesPrice':
			case 'BasicPrice':
			case 'SGMPrice':
			case 'DlDiscountPrice':
			case 'MileagePoint':
			case 'DownLoadSize':
			case 'Postage':
			case 'ProductStock':
			case 'LimitInitial':
			case 'LimitThreshold':
				Value = (Value*1).digitizing();
				if(typeof format !== 'undefined' && format !== null && format.indexOf('{val}') >= 0) Value = format.replace(/\{val\}/ig ,Value);
			break;
			case 'ShipBeginDate':
			case 'SaleStartDate':
			case 'SaleEndDate':
			case 'ApplyStartDate':
			case 'ApplyEndDate':
			case 'SpecialSaleStartDate':
			case 'SpecialSaleEndDate':
				var time = new Date(Value);
				if(typeof format === 'undefined' || format === null) format = 'M月D日（AAA）';
				Value = time.formatt(format);
			break;
			default:
				if(typeof format !== 'undefined' && format !== null) Value = format.replace(/\{val\}/ig ,Value);
			break;
		}
		return Value;
	};
	var attachData = function($elm ,cartInfo){
			var _field = $elm.data('field');
			var _format = $elm.data('field-format');
			if(typeof _field === 'undefined' || _field === '') return true;

			var fields = _field.split('|');
			var formats = (typeof _format === 'undefined' || _format === '')? new Array(fields.length) : _format.toString().split('|');
			
			for(var i=0; fields.length > i; i++) {
				var _field = fields[i];
				var fieldArray = _field.split('.');

				if(typeof fieldArray[0] === 'undefined') continue;
				var field = fieldArray[0].split('/');
				
				var _cartInfo = cartInfo;
				for(var j=0; field.length > j; j++) {
					_cartInfo = _cartInfo[field[j]];
				}
				var value = _cartInfo;
				
				var format = formats[i];

				if (typeof value === 'undefined') return true;

				var attrs = fieldArray[1] || 'innerHTML';
				attrs = attrs.split('/');
				
				var attr = attrs[0].toLowerCase();
				var option = (function(){
					if (attrs.length == 1) return undefined;
					else if (attrs.length == 2) return attrs[1];
					var temp = [];
					for(var i=1; attrs.length>i; i++) {
						temp.push(attrs[i]);
					}
					return temp.join('/');
				})();
				
				var comp = option;
				if (typeof option === 'undefined') comp = undefined;
				else if (option.indexOf('noteq(') >= 0) option = 'noteq';
				else if (option.indexOf('g(') >= 0) option = 'greater';
				else if (option.indexOf('greater(') >= 0) option = 'greater';
				else if(option.indexOf('geq(') >= 0) option = 'greatereq';
				else if(option.indexOf('greatereq(') >= 0) option = 'greatereq';
				else if (option.indexOf('l(') >= 0) option = 'less';
				else if (option.indexOf('less(') >= 0) option = 'less';
				else if(option.indexOf('leq(') >= 0) option = 'lesseq';
				else if(option.indexOf('lesseq(') >= 0) option = 'lesseq';
				else if(option.indexOf('eq(') >= 0) option = 'eq';
				
				if (option === 'eq' || option === 'noteq') {
					comp = comp.match(/.*eq\((.+?)\)/i)[1];
				} else if (option === 'greater' || option === 'greatereq') {
					comp = comp.match(/g.*\((.+?)\)/i)[1];
				} else if (option === 'less' || option === 'lesseq') {
					comp = comp.match(/l.*\((.+?)\)/i)[1];
				}

				var _value = value;
				if (typeof value !== 'undefined' && value !== '' && value !== null) {
					switch (_field.split('.')[0]) {
						case 'SalesPrice':
						case 'BasicPrice':
						case 'SGMPrice':
						case 'DlDiscountPrice':
						case 'MileagePoint':
						case 'DownLoadSize':
						case 'Postage':
						case 'ProductStock':
						case 'LimitInitial':
						case 'LimitThreshold':
							_value = value * 1;
							comp = comp * 1;
							if(isNaN(comp)) comp = undefined;
							break;
						case 'ShipBeginDate':
						case 'SaleStartDate':
						case 'SaleEndDate':
						case 'ApplyStartDate':
						case 'ApplyEndDate':
						case 'SpecialSaleStartDate':
						case 'SpecialSaleEndDate':
							_value = new Date(value).getTime();
							comp = new Date(comp).getTime();
						break;
					}
				}
/*
				console.log(
				{
					field:_field
					, comp:comp
					, value:_value
					, bool : (option === 'lesseq' && comp > _value)
				});
*/
				if (typeof comp === 'undefined') true;
				else if (option === 'eq' && comp !== _value) continue;
				else if (option === 'noteq' && comp === _value) continue;
				else if (option === 'greater' && comp >= _value) continue;
				else if (option === 'greatereq' && comp > _value) continue;
				else if (option === 'less' && comp <= _value) continue;
				else if (option === 'lesseq' && comp < _value) continue;

				switch (attr) {
					case 'bg':
						$elm.css('background-image','url("' + value + '")');
						break;
					case 'class':
						$elm.addClass(getValue(null ,format ,value));
						break;
					case 'addclass':
						if(typeof value !== 'boolean' || typeof option === 'undefined') break;
						var options = option.split('.');
						var myOption = (options.length === 2)? options[0].toString().toLowerCase() : null;
						var myClass = (options.length === 2)? options[1] : options[0];
						
						if (typeof myClass === 'undefined') break;
						
						if(myOption === 'not' && !value) {
							$elm.addClass(myClass);
						} else if (myOption !== 'not' && value) {
							$elm.addClass(myClass);
						}
						
						break;
					case 'checked':
						if (typeof value === 'boolean') $elm.prop('checked',value);
						break;
					case 'selected':
						$elm.prop('selected',value);
						break;
					case 'innerhtml':
					case 'html':
						$elm.html(getValue(_field ,format ,value));
						break;
					default:
						$elm.attr(attr ,getValue(_field ,format ,value));
						break;
				}
			}

	};
	
	return this.each(function() {
		var $this = $(this);

		/*製品コードを取得し、カート情報を定義 製品コードに該当するデータが無ければ処理をスキップ*/
		var code = $this.data('code');//製品コード取得
		var cartInfo = cartInformation[code];//カート情報の定義
		if(typeof cartInfo === 'undefined') return true;//該当するデータが無ければ処理をスキップ

		/*代入が必要なDOMを抽出*/
		var $fields = $this.find('*[data-field]');
		if(cartInfo.BasicPrice === cartInfo.SalesPrice) $this.addClass('zero-difference');
		
		attachData($this ,cartInfo);
		$fields.each(function(){
			attachData($(this) ,cartInfo);
			$(this).removeAttr('data-field');
			$(this).removeAttr('data-field-format');
		});
		$this.removeAttr('data-field');
		$this.removeAttr('data-field-format');
	});
};

//]]>
</script>

                        elm.html(html).attr('data-targettime', targetTime).attr('data-distance', TimerDistance).attr('data-limit', new Date(Deadline.format('YYYY/MM/DD')).getTime()).addClass(className);
                    })(elm, now, Deadline, exclusionDay, shipDate, json.exclusionDays, pattern);


                    if ($('.Distance-countdown').length > 0) {
                        setInterval(function () {

                                var distanceSec, distance, targetTime, currentTime, $this, H, M, S, D, limit;
                                $this = $(this);

                                if (distanceSec <= 0) {
                                    location.reload(true);
                                    return false;

                                    location.reload(true);
                                    return false;
                                }

                                H = Math.floor(distanceSec / (60 * 60 * 1000));

                                S = Math.floor(((distanceSec % (60 * 60 * 1000)) % (60 * 1000)) / 1000);

                            });

            };
            var SSID;
            if(typeof sourcenext.Datas.COOKIE !== 'undefined' && typeof sourcenext.Datas.COOKIE.SN_SSID === 'undefined') SSID = sourcenext.Datas.COOKIE.SN_SSID;
            else SSID = CybozuLabs.MD5.calc(Math.floor(Math.random() * 1000000000) + '-' + getStrNow());
            setCookie('SN_SSID', SSID, 0.25);
            setBeacon("Event=PV&Page=OPEN");
        }
        sourcenext.Flags.setBeacon = true;
    })(jQuery);
//]]>
</script>
